<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:припереть.html>припере́ть</a> (19538)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>пере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припереть.html>припере́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priperétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">припира́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to secure (a door, etc.), to close tightly so it can't be opened</li>
<li>to press (something) firmly against <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">k</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to set ajar (a door, window, etc.)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to carry, to take</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:припереться.html>припере́ться</a> (17342)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припереть.html>припере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priperétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припереться.html>припере́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priperétʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">припира́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">uninvited or inappropriately</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1927</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arkady_Gaidar" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Arkady Gaidar">Arkady Gaidar</a>,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:ударник.html>Уда́рник</a></cite>  | <cite>The shock worker</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">— <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зачем.html>заче́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сюда.html>сюда́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:припереться.html>припёрся</a></b>? <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>чтобы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиде́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дома</a>!</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">— Ty začem sjuda <b>pripjórsja</b>? Ja že tebe govoril, štoby ty sidel doma!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">‘Why did you <b>freaking come</b> here? I told you to stay home!’</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1949</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Feodor_Gladkov" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Feodor Gladkov">Feodor Gladkov</a>,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:повесть.html>По́весть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:детство.html>де́тстве</a></cite>  | <cite>A story of my childhood</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">— <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>Э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> канальи? Поч-чему <b><a href = vnd.unilang:припереться.html>припёрлись</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сюда.html>сюда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> дрючками, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбойник.html>разбо́йники</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>дороги</a>?</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">— Eto što takoje za kanalʹi? Poč-čemu <b>pripjórlisʹ</b> sjuda s drjučkami, kak razbojniki s bolʹšoj dorogi?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">‘Why you little rascals! Why did you <b>freaking come</b> here with your sticks like highwaymen?’</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припереть.html>припере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priperétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приписать.html>приписа́ть</a> (9602)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приписать.html>приписа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pripisátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приписывать.html>припи́сывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to add <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">by writing</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to attach, to register</li>
<li>to arrogate, to ascribe, to attribute, to impute</li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:приподнять.html>приподня́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>при-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-подним-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поднять.html>подня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приподнять.html>приподня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pripodnjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приподнимать.html>приподнима́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приподымать.html>приподыма́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to raise, to lift (a little)</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ня́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 14c/c[①].      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:приподнимать.html>приподнима́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:приподымать.html>приподыма́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;">разг.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> спряжения: <a href = vnd.unilang:наст.html>наст</a>. <i>приподыму́, приподы́мешь…</i>, пов. <i>приподыми́, приподыми́те</i>.

***приподняться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приподняться.html>приподня́ться</a> (5180)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приподнять.html>приподня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pripodnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приподняться.html>приподня́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pripodnjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">приподнима́ться</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">приподыма́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to raise oneself, to lift oneself (a little)</li>
<li>to sit up</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приподнять.html>приподня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pripodnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">приподнима́ние</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pripodnimánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ня́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 14c/c".     <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> прош. вр. муж. <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:возможный.html>возмо́жна</a> устаревающая <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:приподняться.html>приподнялся́</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — приподниматься, приподыматься.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:равноправный.html>равнопра́вно</a> спряжение <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> -ы- <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рне</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:наст.html>наст</a>. вр. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:приподняться.html>приподыму́сь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:приподняться.html>приподы́мешься</a>...</i>, пов. накл. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:приподняться.html>приподыми́сь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:приподняться.html>приподыми́тесь</a></i>.
</p>

***припоминать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:припоминать.html>припомина́ть</a> (9859)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поминать.html>помина́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pominátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to remember, to recall (dated)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припоминать.html>припомина́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pripominátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припомнить.html>припо́мнить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to remember, to recall</li>
<li>to get even, to revenge</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:припомнить.html>припо́мнить</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:припомнить.html>припо́мнивший</a> (5056)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:припомнить.html>припо́мнить</a> (5056)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помнить.html>по́мнить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pómnitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to remember; <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in the negative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to lose control</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припомнить.html>припо́мнить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pripómnitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припоминать.html>припомина́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to remember, to recall</li>
<li>to get even, to revenge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:припомнить.html>припо́мню</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja tebé éto <b>pripómnju</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'll get you for this!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***приправа.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приправа.html>припра́ва</a> (20818)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приправа.html>припра́ва</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pripráva</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приправа.html>припра́вы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приправа.html>припра́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приправа.html>припра́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>seasoning, relish, condiment, flavouring (something used to enhance flavor)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">приправля́ть</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pripravljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">припра́вить</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">priprávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***припрятать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:припрятать.html>припря́тать</a> (15221)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прятать.html>пря́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prjátatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:припрятать.html>припря́тать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priprjátatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">припря́тывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hide, to secrete</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lay up, to store up, to put by</li></ol>
